<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Switch.HiddenInput</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Switch.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">For a controlled Switch component, the state of the toggle is managed using the checked prop, and updates when the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onCheckedChange</code> event handler is called:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the switch is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useSwitch</code> hook. This way you
can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a switch. It includes handling
ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access the switch&#x27;s state with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Switch.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useSwitchContext</code> hook. This lets you customize the component
based on its current state:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="aschild" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#aschild"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>asChild</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Switch.Root</code> element of the switch is a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">label</code> element. This is because the switch is a form control and should be
associated with a label to provide context and meaning to the user. Otherwise, the HTML and accessibility structure will
be invalid.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">If you need to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">asChild</code> property, make sure that the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">label</code> element is the direct child of the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Switch.Root</code>
component.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;label&gt;</code> element.</p><div <h3 id="context-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Complies with the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/switch/" class="link">Switch WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"switch\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cSwitch.Root\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Thumb /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Label /\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/react/switch'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSwitch.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/solid/switch'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSwitch.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/vue/switch'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb :class=\"styles.Thumb\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Switch } from '@ark-ui/svelte/switch'\n  import styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSwitch.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nFor a controlled Switch component, the state of the toggle is managed using the checked prop, and updates when the\n`onCheckedChange` event handler is called:\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/react/switch'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [checked, setChecked] = useState(false)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cSwitch.Root className={styles.Root} checked={checked} onCheckedChange={(e) =\u003e setChecked(e.checked)}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/solid/switch'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [checked, setChecked] = createSignal(false)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cSwitch.Root class={styles.Root} checked={checked()} onCheckedChange={(e) =\u003e setChecked(e.checked)}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/vue/switch'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nconst checked = ref(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model:checked=\"checked\"\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb :class=\"styles.Thumb\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Switch } from '@ark-ui/svelte/switch'\n  import styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\n  let checked = $state(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSwitch.Root class={styles.Root} bind:checked\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the switch is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useSwitch` hook. This way you\ncan access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Switch, useSwitch } from '@ark-ui/react/switch'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const _switch = useSwitch()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e _switch.toggleChecked()}\u003e\n        Toggle\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cSwitch.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={_switch}\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cSwitch.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Switch.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Switch, useSwitch } from '@ark-ui/solid/switch'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const _switch = useSwitch()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e _switch().toggleChecked()}\u003e\n        Toggle\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cSwitch.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={_switch}\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Switch.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Switch, useSwitch } from '@ark-ui/vue/switch'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nconst _switch = useSwitch()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"_switch.toggleChecked()\"\u003eToggle\u003c/button\u003e\n\n    \u003cSwitch.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"_switch\"\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Thumb :class=\"styles.Thumb\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Switch, useSwitch } from '@ark-ui/svelte/switch'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const _switch = useSwitch({ id })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e _switch().toggleChecked()}\u003eToggle\u003c/button\u003e\n\n  \u003cSwitch.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={_switch}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Field\n\nThe `Field` component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a switch. It includes handling\nARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/react/switch'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText className={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText className={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/solid/switch'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/vue/field'\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/vue/switch'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cField.Root :class=\"field.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cSwitch.Thumb :class=\"styles.Thumb\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText :class=\"field.HelperText\"\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText :class=\"field.ErrorText\"\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Field } from '@ark-ui/svelte/field'\n  import { Switch } from '@ark-ui/svelte/switch'\n  import field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n  \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n  \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n\u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Context\n\nAccess the switch's state with `Switch.Context` or the `useSwitchContext` hook. This lets you customize the component\nbased on its current state:\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/react/switch'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSwitch.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Context\u003e\n      {(context) =\u003e (\n        \u003cSwitch.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eFeature is {context.checked ? 'enabled' : 'disabled'}\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/Switch.Context\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/solid/switch'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSwitch.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Context\u003e\n      {(context) =\u003e (\n        \u003cSwitch.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eFeature is {context().checked ? 'enabled' : 'disabled'}\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/Switch.Context\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Switch } from '@ark-ui/vue/switch'\nimport styles from 'styles/switch.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Thumb :class=\"styles.Thumb\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Switch.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSwitch.Context v-slot=\"api\"\u003e\n      \u003cSwitch.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eFeature is {{ api.checked ? 'enabled' : 'disabled'}\u003c/Switch.Label\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/Switch.Context\u003e\n  \u003cSwitch.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/Switch.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n## Guides\n\n### asChild\n\nThe `Switch.Root` element of the switch is a `label` element. This is because the switch is a form control and should be\nassociated with a label to provide context and meaning to the user. Otherwise, the HTML and accessibility structure will\nbe invalid.\n\n\u003e If you need to use the `asChild` property, make sure that the `label` element is the direct child of the `Switch.Root`\n\u003e component.\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `checked` | `boolean` | No | The controlled checked state of the switch |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the switch is disabled. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ root: string; hiddenInput: string; control: string; label: string; thumb: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the switch. Useful for composition. |\n| `invalid` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the switch is marked as invalid. |\n| `label` | `string` | No | Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states |\n| `name` | `string` | No | The name of the input field in a switch\n(Useful for form submission). |\n| `onCheckedChange` | `(details: CheckedChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function to call when the switch is clicked. |\n| `readOnly` | `boolean` | No | Whether the switch is read-only |\n| `required` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the switch input is marked as required, |\n| `value` | `string | number` | No | The value of switch input. Useful for form submission. |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-active]` | Present when active or pressed |\n| `[data-focus]` | Present when
